Some(ctx.key_name().to_string())\n424\t                            );\n425\t                        } else if ctx.is_inline_scalar() {\n426\t                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n427\t                                parse_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n428\t                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n429\t                                    dup_err.message()\n430\t                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n431\t                            }\n432\t                        }\n433\t                    }\n434\t                }\n435\t                Ordering::Equal => {\n436\t                    // Same scope - check for keys\n437\t                    if let Some(ctx) = extract_key_context(line) {\n438\t                        if ctx.is_parent_key() {\n439\t                            // This is a sibling parent key at same indent level\n440\t                            // Exit and re-enter scope for the sibling\n441\t                            #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n442\t                            {\n443\t                                log_debug!(\"[parse_str] Sibling parent key: key='{}', indent={}, line={}\",\n444\t                                    ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index);\n445\t                            }\n446\t                            scope_stack.exit_to_scope(indent);\n447\t                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n448\t                                parse_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n449\t                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n450\t                                    dup_err.message()\n451\t                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n452\t                            }\n453\t                            #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n454\t                            {\n455\t                                log_debug!(\"[parse_str] Re-entering scope: type=Mapping, key='{}', indent={}, line={}\",\n456\t                                    ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index);\n457\t                            }\n458\t                            scope_stack.enter_scope(\n459\t                                indent + scope_stack.base_indent(),\n460\t                                line_num_1index,\n461\t                                Some(ctx.key_name().to_string())\n462\t                            );\n463\t                        } else if ctx.is_inline_scalar() {\n464\t                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n465\t                                parse_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n466\t                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n467\t                                    dup_err.message()\n468\t                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n469\t                            }\n470\t                        }\n471\t                    }\n472\t                }\n473\t            }\n474\t\n475\t            // Handle sequence items with their own scopes\n476\t            if trimmed.starts_with(\"- \") {\n477\t                if let Some(ctx) = extract_key_context(line) {\n478\t                    // Enter a sequence scope for this item\n479\t                    log_debug!(\"DEBUG [parse_str]: Entering sequence scope for key '{}' at indent {} on line {}\",\n480\t                        ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index);\n481\t                    scope_stack.enter_sequence_scope(indent, line_num_1index);\n482\t                    // Add the key to the sequence scope\n483\t                    if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n484\t                        parse_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n485\t                            format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n486\t                            dup_err.message()\n487\t                        ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n488\t                    }\n489\t                } else {\n490\t                    // Sequence item without a key context\n491\t                    log_debug!(\"DEBUG [parse_str]: Entering sequence scope (no key) at indent {} on line {}\",\n492\t                        indent, line_num_1index);\n493\t                    scope_stack.enter_sequence_scope(indent, line_num_1index);\n494\t                }\n495\t            }\n496\t        }\n497\t\n498\t        // Return parse result using serde_yaml for the actual value\n499\t        match serde_yaml::from_str::<serde_yaml::Value>(content) {\n500\t            Ok(value) => {\n501\t                // Note: parse_errors from scope tracking are currently informational\n502\t                // They could be added as warnings in a future enhancement\n503\t                ParseResult::success(value)\n504\t            }\n505\t            Err(err) => {\n506\t                // Add any duplicate key errors we found to the parse error\n507\t                let error_msg = if parse_errors.is_empty() {\n508\t                    err.to_string()\n509\t                } else {\n510\t                    format!(\"{}; duplicate key errors: {}\", err, parse_errors.iter()\n511\t                        .map(|e| e.message.clone()).collect::<Vec<_>>().join(\"; \"))\n512\t                };\n513\t                ParseResult::failure(ParseError::syntax(error_msg))\n514\t            }\n515\t        }\n516\t    }\n517\t\n518\t    fn parse_bytes(&self, content: &[u8]) -> ParseResult<serde_yaml::Value> {\n519\t        // Convert bytes to string and parse\n520\t        match std::str::from_utf8(content) {\n521\t            Ok(utf8_content) => self.parse_str(utf8_content),\n522\t            Err(err) => ParseResult::failure(ParseError::io(format!(\"Invalid UTF-8: {}\", err))),\n523\t        }\n524\t    }\n525\t\n526\t    fn parse_file(&self, path: &std::path::Path) -> ParseResult<serde_yaml::Value> {\n527\t        // Read file content\n528\t        match std::fs::read_to_string(path) {\n529\t            Ok(content) => self.parse_str(&content),\n530\t            Err(err) => ParseResult::failure(ParseError::io(format!(\"Failed to read file {}: {}\", path.display(), err))),\n531\t        }\n532\t    }\n533\t\n534\t    fn validate_str(&self, content: &str) -> ValidationResult {\n535\t        // Create syntax validator based on parser mode\n536\t        let validator = if self.config.is_strict() {\n537\t            SyntaxValidator::strict()\n538\t        } else {\n539\t            SyntaxValidator::lenient()\n540\t        };\n541\t\n542\t        // Run syntax validation\n543\t        let mut result = validator.validate(content);\n544\t\n545\t        // Run scope-aware duplicate key detection (when duplicates are not allowed)\n546\t        if !self.config.allow_duplicates {\n547\t            let mut scope_stack = self.scope_stack.clone();\n548\t            let duplicate_errors = self.detect_duplicate_keys_with_scope(content, &mut scope_stack);\n549\t            if !duplicate_errors.is_empty() {\n550\t                result.valid = false;\n551\t                result.errors.extend(duplicate_errors);\n552\t            }\n553\t        }\n554\t\n555\t        // If no errors from basic validation, run enhanced detection\n556\t        if result.is_valid() {\n557\t            let mut detector = SyntaxDetector::new();\n558\t            let detector_result = detector.detect_to_validation_result(content);\n559\t\n560\t            // Merge errors from detector\n561\t            if !detector_result.is_valid() {\n562\t                result.valid = false;\n563\t                result.errors.extend(detector_result.errors);\n564\t            }\n565\t        }\n566\t\n567\t        result\n568\t    }\n569\t\n570\t    fn validate_file(&self, path: &std::path::Path) -> ValidationResult {\n571\t        // Read file content\n572\t        let content = match std::fs::read_to_string(path) {\n573\t            Ok(content) => content,\n574\t            Err(err) => {\n575\t                return ValidationResult {\n576\t                    valid: false,\n577\t                    errors: vec![ValidationError::new(\n578\t                        path.display().to_string(),\n579\t                        format!(\"failed to read file: {}\", err)\n580\t                    )],\n581\t                    warnings: Vec::new(),\n582\t                };\n583\t            }\n584\t        };\n585\t\n586\t        // Validate the content\n587\t        self.validate_str(&content)\n588\t    }\n589\t\n590\t    fn config(&self) -> &ParserConfig {\n591\t        &self.config\n592\t    }\n593\t\n594\t    fn with_config(self, config: ParserConfig) -> Self\n595\t    where\n596\t        Self: Sized,\n597\t    {\n598\t        Self {\n599\t            config,\n600\t            scope_stack: ScopeStack::new(2), // Standard 2-space YAML indentation\n601\t        }\n602\t    }\n603\t}\n604\t\n605\t// ============================================================================\n606\t// Integration Tests for Scope Tracking\n607\t// continue;\n            }\n\n            // Skip YAML directives\n            if trimmed.starts_with('%') {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            let indent = calculate_indentation(line);\n\n            // Handle scope transitions based on indentation changes\n            use std::cmp::Ordering;\n            match indent.cmp(&scope_stack.current_indent()) {\n                Ordering::Greater => {\n                    // Indent increased - entering deeper scope\n                    if let Some(ctx) = extract_key_context(line) {\n dup_err.message()\n                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                            }\n                            // Enter new scope for the parent key's nested content\n file content\n        match std::fs::read_to_string(path) {\n            Ok(content) => self.parse_str(&content),\n            Err(err) => ParseResult::failure(ParseError::io(format!(\"Failed to read      result.valid = false;\n                result.errors.extend(duplicate_errors);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // If no errors from basic validation, run enhanced detection\n        if result.is_valid() {\n            let mut detector = SyntaxDetector::new();\n            let detector_result = detector.detect_to_validation_result(content);\n\n            // Merge errors from detector\n            if !detector_result.is_valid() {\n                result.valid = false;\n                result.errors.extend(detector_result.errors);\n            }\n        }\n\n        result\n    }\n\n    fn validate_file(&self, path: &std::path::Path) -> ValidationResult {\n        // Read file content\n        let content = match std::fs::read_to_string(path) {\n            Ok(content) => content,\n            Err(err) => {\n                return ValidationResult {\n                    valid: false,\n                    errors: vec![ValidationError::new(\n                        path.display().to_string(),\n                        format!(\"failed to read file: {}\", err)\n                    )],\n                    warnings: Vec::new(),\n                };\n            }\n        };\n\n        // Validate the content\n        self.validate_str(&content)\n    }\n\n    fn config(&self) -> &ParserConfig {\n        &self.config\n    }\n\n    fn with_config(self, Core parser trait and implementations for YAML parsing\n//!\n//! This module defines the Parser trait and provides functionality for\n//! parsing YAML content from various sources.\n\nuse crate::parsers::yaml::{\n    types::{ParseResult, ValidationResult, ValidationError},\n    error::ParseError,\n    ParserConfig,\n    syntax_validator::SyntaxValidator,\n    syntax_detector::SyntaxDetector,\n    scope::ScopeStack,\n    line_parser::{calculate_indentation},\n    scope::extract_key_context,\n};\n\n#[cfg(debug_assertions)]\nuse log::debug as log_debug;\n#[cfg(debug_assertions)]\nuse log::warn as log_warn;\n\n/// Trait for YAML parsers\n///\n/// This trait defines the core interface for parsing YAML content.\n/// Implementations can parse from strings, files, or other sources.\npub trait Parser {\n    /// Parse YAML content from a string\n    ///\n    /// # Arguments\n    /// * `content` - The YAML content as a string\n    ///\n    /// # Returns\n    /// A ParseResult containing the parsed data or an error\n    fn parse_str(&self, content: &str) -> ParseResult<serde_yaml::Value>;\n\n    /// Parse YAML content from a byte slice\n    fn parse_bytes(&self, content: &[u8]) -> ParseResult<serde_yaml::Value>;\n\n    /// Parse YAML content from a file\n    fn parse_file(&self, path: &std::path::Path) -> ParseResult<serde_yaml::Value>;\n\n    /// Validate YAML content without fully parsing it\n    fn validate_str(&self, content: &str) -> ValidationResult;\n\n    /// Validate a YAML file without fully parsing it\n    fn validate_file(&self, path: &std::path::Path) -> ValidationResult;\n\n    /// Get the parser configuration\n    ///\n    /// # Returns\n    /// A reference to the parser's configuration\n    fn config(&self) -> &ParserConfig;\n\n    /// Set the parser configuration\n    ///\n    /// # Arguments\n    /// * `config` - The new configuration\n    ///\n    /// # Returns\n    /// The parser with the new configuration\n    fn with_config(self, config: ParserConfig) -> Self\n    where\n        Self: Sized;\n}\n\n/// Basic YAML parser implementation\n///\n/// This is a minimal implementation of the Parser trait that\n/// provides basic YAML parsing functionality with scope-aware key tracking.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct BasicParser {\n    config: ParserConfig,\n    /// Scope stack for tracking keys within their proper scope contexts\n    scope_stack: ScopeStack,\n}\n\nimpl BasicParser {\n    /// Create a new BasicParser with default configuration\n    pub fn new() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            config: ParserConfig::default(),\n            scope_stack: ScopeStack::new(2), // Standard 2-space YAML indentation\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Create a new BasicParser with the specified configuration\n    pub fn with_config(config: ParserConfig) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            config,\n            scope_stack: ScopeStack::new(2), // Standard 2-space YAML indentation\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Create a new strict parser\n    ///\n    /// A strict parser enables strict mode and disallows duplicate keys.\n    /// Uses the comprehensive strict configuration from ParserConfig.\n    pub fn strict() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            config: ParserConfig::strict(),\n            scope_stack: ScopeStack::new(2), // Standard 2-space YAML indentation\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Detect duplicate keys using scope-aware tracking\n    ///\n    /// This method processes YAML content line-by-line, tracking keys within\n    /// their proper scope contexts. It returns a list of validation errors\n    /// for any duplicate keys found within the same scope.\n    fn detect_duplicate_keys_with_scope(&self, content: &str, scope_stack: &mut ScopeStack) -> Vec<ValidationError> {\n        let mut duplicate_errors = Vec::new();\n\n        for (line_num, line) in content.lines().enumerate() {\n            let line_num_1index = line_num + 1;\n            let trimmed = line.trim();\n\n            // Skip empty lines and comments\n            if trimmed.is_empty() || trimmed.starts_with('#') {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            // Handle document markers - reset scope tracking\n            if trimmed == \"---\" || trimmed == \"...\" {\n                #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                {\n                    log_debug!(\"[detect_duplicate] Document marker '{}' at line={}, resetting scope stack\", trimmed, line_num_1index);\n                }\n                scope_stack.reset();\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            // Skip YAML directives\n            if trimmed.starts_with('%') {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            let indent = calculate_indentation(line);\n\n            // Handle scope transitions based on indentation changes\n            use std::cmp::Ordering;\n            match indent.cmp(&scope_stack.current_indent()) {\n                Ordering::Greater => {\n                    // Indent increased - entering deeper scope\n                    if let Some(ctx) = extract_key_context(line) {\n                        if ctx.is_parent_key() {\n                            // Add the parent key to current scope\n                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                                duplicate_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                                    dup_err.message()\n                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                            }\n                            // Enter new scope for the parent key's nested content\n                            #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                            {\n                                log_debug!(\"[detect_duplicate] Entering scope: type=Mapping, key='{}', indent={}, line={}\",\n                                    ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index);\n                            }\n                            scope_stack.enter_scope(\n                                indent + scope_stack.base_indent(),\n                                line_num_1index,\n                                Some(ctx.key_name().to_string())\n                            );\n                        } else {\n                            // Indent increased but not a parent key - this is an inline scalar at deeper indent\n                            // Just add the key to current scope, don't create a new scope\n                            #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                            {\n                                log_debug!(\"[detect_duplicate] Inline scalar: key='{}', indent={}, line={}, in_sequence={}\",\n                                    ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index, scope_stack.in_sequence_context());\n                            }\n                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                                duplicate_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                                    dup_err.message()\n                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                            }\n                        }\n                    } else {\n                        // Indent increased but no key context found - this is likely:\n                        // - A sequence item continuation (already handled by sequence scope logic)\n                        // - A scalar value continuation\n                        // - Don't enter a scope for non-key lines\n                        #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                        {\n                            log_debug!(\"[detect_duplicate] No key context: line={}, indent={}, in_sequence={}, skipping scope entry\",\n                                line_num_1index, indent, scope_stack.in_sequence_context());\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                Ordering::Less => {\n                    // Indent decreased - exit to parent scope\n                    #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                    {\n                        log_debug!(\"[detect_duplicate] Scope exit: from_indent={}, to_indent={}, line={}\",\n                            scope_stack.current_indent(), indent, line_num_1index);\n                    }\n                    scope_stack.exit_to_scope(indent);\n\n                    // After exiting, check if this line has a key\n                    if let Some(ctx) = extract_key_context(line) {\n                        if ctx.is_parent_key() {\n                            // This is a new parent key at this level\n                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                                duplicate_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                                    dup_err.message()\n                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                            }\n                            #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                            {\n                                log_debug!(\"[detect_duplicate] Entering scope: type=Mapping, key='{}', indent={}, line={}\",\n                                    ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index);\n                            }\n                            scope_stack.enter_scope(\n                                indent + scope_stack.base_indent(),\n                                line_num_1index,\n                                Some(ctx.key_name().to_string())\n                            );\n                        } else if ctx.is_inline_scalar() {\n                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                                duplicate_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                                    dup_err.message()\n                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                    // Edge case: indent decreased but no key - we've already exited to the right scope\n                }\n                Ordering::Equal => {\n                    // Same scope - check for keys\n                    if let Some(ctx) = extract_key_context(line) {\n                        if ctx.is_parent_key() {\n                            // This is a sibling parent key at same indent level\n                            // Exit and re-enter scope for the sibling\n                            #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                            {\n                                log_debug!(\"[detect_duplicate] Sibling parent key: key='{}', indent={}, line={}\",\n                                    ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index);\n                            }\n                            scope_stack.exit_to_scope(indent);\n                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                                duplicate_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                                    dup_err.message()\n                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                            }\n                            #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                            {\n                                log_debug!(\"[detect_duplicate] Re-entering scope: type=Mapping, key='{}', indent={}, line={}\",\n                                    ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index);\n                            }\n                            scope_stack.enter_scope(\n                                indent + scope_stack.base_indent(),\n                                line_num_1index,\n                                Some(ctx.key_name().to_string())\n                            );\n                        } else if ctx.is_inline_scalar() {\n                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                                duplicate_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                                    dup_err.message()\n                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                    // Edge case: same indent but no key - just continue, no scope change needed\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Handle sequence items with their own scopes\n            if trimmed.starts_with(\"- \") {\n                if let Some(ctx) = extract_key_context(line) {\n                    // Enter a sequence scope for this item\n                    #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                    {\n                        log_debug!(\"[detect_duplicate] Entering scope: type=Sequence, key='{}', indent={}, line={}\",\n                            ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index);\n                    }\n                    scope_stack.enter_sequence_scope(indent, line_num_1index);\n                    // Add the key to the sequence scope\n                    if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                        duplicate_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                            format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                            dup_err.message()\n                        ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    // Sequence item without a key context\n                    #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                    {\n                        log_debug!(\"[detect_duplicate] Entering scope: type=Sequence (no key), indent={}, line={}\",\n                            indent, line_num_1index);\n                    }\n                    scope_stack.enter_sequence_scope(indent, line_num_1index);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        duplicate_errors\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Default for BasicParser {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self::new()\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Parser for BasicParser {\n    fn parse_str(&self, content: &str) -> ParseResult<serde_yaml::Value> {\n        // Create a new scope stack for this parsing operation\n        let mut scope_stack = ScopeStack::new(2);\n        let mut parse_errors = Vec::new();\n\n        // Parse line by line with scope-aware key tracking\n        for (line_num, line) in content.lines().enumerate() {\n            let line_num_1index = line_num + 1;\n            let trimmed = line.trim();\n\n            // Skip empty lines and comments for key tracking\n            if trimmed.is_empty() || trimmed.starts_with('#') {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            // Handle document markers - reset scope tracking\n            if trimmed == \"---\" || trimmed == \"...\" {\n                #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                {\n                    log_debug!(\"[parse_str] Document marker '{}' at line={}, resetting scope stack\", trimmed, line_num_1index);\n                }\n                scope_stack.reset();\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            // Skip YAML directives\n            if trimmed.starts_with('%') {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            let indent = calculate_indentation(line);\n\n            // Handle scope transitions based on indentation changes\n            use std::cmp::Ordering;\n            match indent.cmp(&scope_stack.current_indent()) {\n                Ordering::Greater => {\n                    // Indent increased - entering deeper scope\n                    if let Some(ctx) = extract_key_context(line) {\n                        if ctx.is_parent_key() {\n                            // Add the parent key to current scope\n                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                                parse_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                                    dup_err.message()\n                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                            }\n                            // Enter new scope for the parent key's nested content\n                            #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                            {\n                                log_debug!(\"[parse_str] Entering scope: type=Mapping, key='{}', indent={}, line={}\",\n                                    ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index);\n                            }\n                            scope_stack.enter_scope(\n                                indent + scope_stack.base_indent(),\n                                line_num_1index,\n                                Some(ctx.key_name().to_string())\n                            );\n                        } else {\n                            // Indent increased but not a parent key - this is an inline scalar at deeper indent\n                            // Just add the key to current scope, don't create a new scope\n                            #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                            {\n                                log_debug!(\"[parse_str] Inline scalar: key='{}', indent={}, line={}, in_sequence={}\",\n                                    ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index, scope_stack.in_sequence_context());\n                            }\n                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                                parse_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                                    dup_err.message()\n                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                            }\n                        }\n                    } else {\n                        // Indent increased but no key context found - this is likely:\n                        // - A sequence item continuation (already handled by sequence scope logic)\n                        // - A scalar value continuation\n                        // - Don't enter a scope for non-key lines\n                        #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                        {\n                            log_debug!(\"[parse_str] No key context: line={}, indent={}, in_sequence={}, skipping scope entry\",\n                                line_num_1index, indent, scope_stack.in_sequence_context());\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                Ordering::Less => {\n                    // Indent decreased - exit to parent scope\n                    #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                    {\n                        log_debug!(\"[parse_str] Scope exit: from_indent={}, to_indent={}, line={}\",\n                            scope_stack.current_indent(), indent, line_num_1index);\n                    }\n                    scope_stack.exit_to_scope(indent);\n\n                    // After exiting, check if this line has a key\n                    if let Some(ctx) = extract_key_context(line) {\n                        if ctx.is_parent_key() {\n                            // This is a new parent key at this level\n                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                                parse_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                                    dup_err.message()\n                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                            }\n                            #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                            {\n                                log_debug!(\"[parse_str] Entering scope: type=Mapping, key='{}', indent={}, line={}\",\n                                    ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index);\n                            }\n                            scope_stack.enter_scope(\n                                indent + scope_stack.base_indent(),\n                                line_num_1index,\n                                Some(ctx.key_name().to_string())\n                            );\n                        } else if ctx.is_inline_scalar() {\n                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                                parse_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                                    dup_err.message()\n                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                Ordering::Equal => {\n                    // Same scope - check for keys\n                    if let Some(ctx) = extract_key_context(line) {\n                        if ctx.is_parent_key() {\n                            // This is a sibling parent key at same indent level\n                            // Exit and re-enter scope for the sibling\n                            #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                            {\n                                log_debug!(\"[parse_str] Sibling parent key: key='{}', indent={}, line={}\",\n                                    ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index);\n                            }\n                            scope_stack.exit_to_scope(indent);\n                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                                parse_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                                    dup_err.message()\n                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                            }\n                            #[cfg(debug_assertions)]\n                            {\n                                log_debug!(\"[parse_str] Re-entering scope: type=Mapping, key='{}', indent={}, line={}\",\n                                    ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index);\n                            }\n                            scope_stack.enter_scope(\n                                indent + scope_stack.base_indent(),\n                                line_num_1index,\n                                Some(ctx.key_name().to_string())\n                            );\n                        } else if ctx.is_inline_scalar() {\n                            if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                                parse_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                                    format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                                    dup_err.message()\n                                ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Handle sequence items with their own scopes\n            if trimmed.starts_with(\"- \") {\n                if let Some(ctx) = extract_key_context(line) {\n                    // Enter a sequence scope for this item\n                    log_debug!(\"DEBUG [parse_str]: Entering sequence scope for key '{}' at indent {} on line {}\",\n                        ctx.key_name(), indent, line_num_1index);\n                    scope_stack.enter_sequence_scope(indent, line_num_1index);\n                    // Add the key to the sequence scope\n                    if let Err(dup_err) = scope_stack.add_key(ctx.key_name(), line_num_1index) {\n                        parse_errors.push(ValidationError::new(\n                            format!(\"line_{}\", line_num_1index),\n                            dup_err.message()\n                        ).with_line(line_num_1index));\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    // Sequence item without a key context\n                    log_debug!(\"DEBUG [parse_str]: Entering sequence scope (no key) at indent {} on line {}\",\n                        indent, line_num_1index);\n                    scope_stack.enter_sequence_scope(indent, line_num_1index);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Return parse result using serde_yaml for the actual value\n        match serde_yaml::from_str::<serde_yaml::Value>(content) {\n            Ok(value) => {\n                // Note: parse_errors from scope tracking are currently informational\n                // They could be added as warnings in a future enhancement\n                ParseResult::success(value)\n            }\n            Err(err) => {\n                // Add any duplicate key errors we found to the parse error\n                let error_msg = if parse_errors.is_empty() {\n                    err.to_string()\n                } else {\n                    format!(\"{}; duplicate key errors: {}\", err, parse_errors.iter()\n                        .map(|e| e.message.clone()).collect::<Vec<_>>().join(\"; \"))\n                };\n                ParseResult::failure(ParseError::syntax(error_msg))\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn parse_bytes(&self, content: &[u8]) -> ParseResult<serde_yaml::Value> {\n        // Convert bytes to string and parse\n        match std::str::from_utf8(content) {\n            Ok(utf8_content) => self.parse_str(utf8_content),\n            Err(err) => ParseResult::failure(ParseError::io(format!(\"Invalid UTF-8: {}\", err))),\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn parse_file(&self, path: &std::path::Path) -> ParseResult<serde_yaml::Value> {\n        // Read file content\n        match std::fs::read_to_string(path) {\n            Ok(content) => self.parse_str(&content),\n            Err(err) => ParseResult::failure(ParseError::io(format!(\"Failed to read file {}: {}\", path.display(), err))),\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn validate_str(&self, content: &str) -> ValidationResult {\n        // Create syntax validator based on parser mode\n        let validator = if self.config.is_strict() {\n            SyntaxValidator::strict()\n        } else {\n            SyntaxValidator::lenient()\n        };\n\n        // Run syntax validation\n        let mut result = validator.validate(content);\n\n        // Run scope-aware duplicate key detection (when duplicates are not allowed)\n        if !self.config.allow_duplicates {\n            let mut scope_stack = self.scope_stack.clone();\n            let duplicate_errors = self.detect_duplicate_keys_with_scope(content, &mut scope_stack);\n            if !duplicate_errors.is_empty() {\n                result.valid = false;\n                result.errors.extend(duplicate_errors);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // If no errors from basic validation, run enhanced detection\n        if result.is_valid() {\n            let mut detector = SyntaxDetector::new();\n            let detector_result = detector.detect_to_validation_result(content);\n\n            // Merge errors from detector\n            if !detector_result.is_valid() {\n                result.valid = false;\n                result.errors.extend(detector_result.errors);\n            }\n        }\n\n        result\n    }\n\n    fn validate_file(&self, path: &std::path::Path) -> ValidationResult {\n        // Read file content\n        let content = match std::fs::read_to_string(path) {\n            Ok(content) => content,\n            Err(err) => {\n                return ValidationResult {\n                    valid: false,\n                    errors: vec![ValidationError::new(\n                        path.display().to_string(),\n                        format!(\"failed to read file: {}\", err)\n                    )],\n                    warnings: Vec::new(),\n                };\n            }\n        };\n\n        // Validate the content\n        self.validate_str(&content)\n    }\n\n    fn config(&self) -> &ParserConfig {\n        &self.config\n    }\n\n    fn with_config(self, config: ParserConfig) -> Self\n    where\n        Self: Sized,\n    {\n        Self {\n            config,\n            scope_stack: ScopeStack::new(2), // Standard 2-space YAML indentation\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// ============================================================================\n// Integration Tests for Scope Tracking\n// ============================================================================\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod integration_tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    /// Test parse_str with nested YAML structures\n    #[test]\n    fn test_parse_str_with_nested_yaml() {\n        let parser = BasicParser::new();\n        let yaml = r#\"\nservices:\n  web:\n    host: localhost\n    port: 8080\n  database:\n    host: db.example.com\n    port: 5432\n\"#;\n\n        let result = parser.parse_str(yaml);\n        assert!(result.is_success(), \"Should parse valid nested YAML successfully\");\n\n        // Verify we can access the parsed structure\n        let value = result.unwrap();\n        assert!(value.is_mapping());\n        assert!(value.get(\"services\").is_some());\n    }\n\n    /// Test parse_str with timeouts:\n        connect: 30\n        read: 60\n    logging:\n      level: info\n  database:\n    connection:\n      pool:\n        max: 10\n        min: 2\n\"#;\n\n        let result =
